<UserId.>115720073075390332991< /UserId.>< Review>
The park is cool, it's decent, the bowl is better then most around. Good park to just skate, nothing too crazy though. Unfortunately you do have to pay for lights with quarters only, which is ridiculous because the parking lot lights stay lit all night. Sometimes the gate gets unlocked around 8am in summer months, sometimes the maintenance guy don't show up till 11am!.  Most of the people who come here are generally nice, restrooms aren't very nice for the females. There are a lot of local skaters who skate here regularly, and unfortunately there's also a lot of small kids who get dropped off while their mom or dad sits in the car. Most of the smaller kids here don't watch out for other riders, they Mostly go in circles and cut in front of everybody. While their parents just watch, and honestly whenever someone tells one of these kids to watch out for others, that's when their parent comes into the park usually trying to intimidate other kids. Please learn to ride whatever it is that you choose at home before going to skateparks, it's helps everyone. Parents should know better when they see their kid playing in the bowl while everybody's waiting to actually ride it, and get em out, these parks aren't playgrounds......J.D.üõπüõπüõπüçÉüçª< /Review>

< Text>
SKATEPARK REVIEW ONLY:BMX PERSPECTIVE:
This park is not a bad park at all. It's not the best  Ut if your within 2 hrs which is kinda pushing it. It's worth a trip. The bowl has some nice vert that once you get comfortable can be very nice. Bowl to bowl spine is moderate size, bigger than most places about 5ish feet maybe bigger but its steepish. The taller quarter in the street section is nice for airing out as well. All in all it's a great little park to get creative and have some fun. I was told that the lights no longer work, THESE ARE LIES LOL THE LIGHTS WORK. you have to pay for it though, I assume if your quarters dont work right away, try try try. It spits them out the bottom if it doesn't go through. You'll find a few riders from time to time. COME OUT AND RIDE!!< /Text>

< review>
This location is experiencing growing pains at least I hope.

Food quality was on par to other CFAs so the star rating is relative to better experiences.

Arrived at the start of lunch time rush, line inside was only halfway to the door but still only had two cashiers working. 10 mins to put in order and 16 mins to receive food, seems like the norm as there were plenty of people sitting and waiting for their food. By the time I left, line was to the door and drive thru line had overflowed onto the street, which along with blocking traffic also blocks those that just want to park in the parking lot.

I plan to reassess in the future to see if improvements have been made.

4/14/20 Update: while their setup for curbside pick up, I beat the lunch time rush and my order came out incorrect. Ordered and paid for spicy chicken sandwich but received an original chicken sandwich< /review>
